04260337760077;Humintech GmbH;PERLHUMUS® Granules is a high quality humic material soil conditioner (Leonardite) which acts as a natural chelator. It consists of immediately available nutrient humus and high quality permanent humus, which cannot be easily decomposed by soil microorganisms. German Leonardite (highly oxidized lignite) is a natural raw material containing a high content of humic matter (humic acid and fulvic acid). Leonardit is formed in specific Sedimentation layers of oxidized soft brown coal which did not reach the stage of brown coal. It arises from the chemical and biological humification of plants and other organic matter, by biological activity and geological processes.;3779
